padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2071768">dudegetsmoney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-07">10/07/24 11:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yes, it's me again, the greatest reviewer of all time (self proclaimed).<br />
<br />
Initially I absolutely loved this. But I think that was because I kept on mixing Symphony and AS with this (I kept testing the three together). But after testing it out a few more times individually, and on skin, I've decided that it really isn't that great.100% agree with the people that said this should've been named On the Beach instead. The opening is a massively bitter citrus that lasts for a whole 10 mins and goes into the middle notes, which smell exactly like sunscreen. There's a bit of citrus bitterness in the background still, and the sandalwood starts to show, but the sunscreen scent is undeniable. And yes, I unfortunately also get Soleil Blanc from this - smells like smoother SB with sweet/bitter citrus. I also did not like Soleil Blanc much...<br />
<br />
It's a powdery, soft dry down that very quickly becomes a skin scent. You'll probably honestly get more projection with sunscreen. It's very pleasant, and I do really like it. But for the same price, the other LVs are just a lot better.<br />
<br />
This does incredibly well when layered with other LVs. like Afternoon Swim and Symphony, but I simply can't justify buying this when AS, PC and Imagination exists.<br />
<br />
For now unfortunately, this will be removed from my to-buy list :(<br />
<br />
7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="2307910"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=2307910#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2306692" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I tend to like fresh, summery fragrances, and this one definitely fits that profile. The citrus opening is so nice, followed by my favorite musk I've ever encountered. The only con is that it doesn't project or last long unless you spray a lot. I think it's overpriced for how long it lasts, but still one of my favorites.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="2279803"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=2279803#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276077" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Phenomenal opening and drydown, so much that I believe it is far better than Imagination.  This one is very mass appealing, it's citrus, and it smells like insanely high quality, expensive citrus at that. <br />
<br />
This fragrance is overshadowed by Imagination, but I personally believe this is way better. The performance is so good that it lasted 8+ hours on my skin, and when I put it on a test strip and I gathered it with my other many test strips, it overpowered every other one, and every single test strip just smelt like this. <br />
<br />
All LV fragrances have good sillage...but some of them experience poor longevity, like Afternoon Swim, and Imagination. I'm glad this one is underrated, and you could gatekeep it if you wanted to but with that price it gatekeeps itself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="2217076"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=2217076#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2215991" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2213937" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JoyDivision"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1580180"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1580180.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JoyDivision" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Lost-Cherry-51411.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.51411.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Lost Cherry"title="Lost Cherry"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2213937ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2213937" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1580180">JoyDivision</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-10">07/10/24 05:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've been looking for a well-balanced summer perfume, something that is sweet and tropical with a good dose of tiare but not something cheap and synthetic that will make me smell like all the 16yo girls waiting to get the bus to the beach. I wanted it to be sophisticated but not smelling like 'mature-lady-on-the-look-out' style. Thank you dear Louis Vuitton because you grand me that wish and made City of Stars. I understand that this perfume depends totally on your skin's chemistry, so on me it starts super citrusy and sweet but not jammy. In about 30 minutes the citrus melts into a well-blended citrus-tiare, almost coconut, powdery scent. It's a compliment magnet and it blooms under the hot Mediterranean sun. Highly recommended!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="2213937"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=2213937#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2205917" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I have also tested TF Soleil Blanc in the past, and that is weaker and not as sweet as Terracotta.  City of stars is powdery, but not toooooo powdery to the point where I wouldn't like it. Mixed with the citrus and tiare it offers a fresher take on the sunscreen vibe, and the sandalwood in the base gives it a nice bit of something extra, maybe even adding a touch of very mild spice, almost a hippy vibe in more of a boho kinda way. The citrus in City of stars is bitter rather than fresh and it's powdery.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="2070682"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=2070682#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2061582" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; In the end the citrusy notes only lasted about an hour and a half on me. <br />
<br />
Once the initial citrusy blast had faded, the sweet and slightly fruity and tropical white flower known as tiare began to unfurl deliciously on my skin and envelop me. I could get a good dose of the musk as well followed by the powdery notes and the sandalwood in that order, but the tiare flower in this was really what shone to me.<br />
<br />
I feel like I'm on a tropical vacation in the Pacific Islands in this and it makes me feel like a tropical island goddess. This is why I definitely think a woman could wear it during the day in both spring and especially summer.<br />
<br />
Heures D'Absence had a moderate sillage on me and it lasted on my skin for  about 10 hours surprisingly. Because of this and the rest above, I'd give this perfume an excellent 8/10. City of Stars is a more subtle luxury IMO, and the citrus is done so well. I love the juxtaposition of juicy citrus, tiare, powder, and sandalwood; it's very clever of Mr. Cavallier. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1880866" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RGH01"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1331188.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RGH01" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1880866ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1880866" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-17">07/17/23 13:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>City of Stars is an ode to the excitement and extravagance of Los Angeles as the sun begins to set. It opens with an intoxicating medley of high quality citrus, most prominently lime and blood orange. A unique note of Tiare is then used which adds that classic white floral touch, with a fruity nuance to it.<br />
<br />
From here, the citrus stays constant as it begins to settle on a powdery base of musk and sandalwood. The sharpness of the citrus perfectly juxtaposes the creaminess of the sandalwood and expresses brilliantly the shift towards dusk. <br />
<br />
I find this fragrance leans slightly feminine but is still wearable by both sexes. It’s a very pleasant and high quality citrus, perfect for the summer however the performance is lacking and it’s severely overpriced for what it is.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Makes it very tropical without being common or ordinary. <br />
No suntan lotion to my nose, it's way more classy and refined.<br />
I like it a lot, wearing it makes me think of KL Fleur d'Orchidée mixed with Girl in Capri (or Lemon Dulci plus bergamot), and a hint of Bronze Goddess.<br />
Extremely pleasant and wearable, good for the office, makes you feel clean and confident and in a summer positive mood. <br />
Alas, longevity is scarce and for that reason i wouldn't go for that pricey full bottle but that's just me; however consider it in case you stumble on a bargain.<br />
Recommend.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="1864941"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=1864941#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1847457" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1556937" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Vannamae__"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1236771"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1236771.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Vannamae__" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Villa-Erbatium/Allegria-98938.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.98938.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Allegria"title="Allegria"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1556937ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1556937" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1236771">Vannamae__</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-04">05/04/22 10:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yes, most perfumes are overpriced from this house, you’re paying for a name after all but I’ve been on the hunt for a beach vibe scent that doesn’t just smell like straight up sun tan lotion which has been challenging until this came into my life. There is a little sun tan lotion effect towards the end of the fragrance but in a good way, not a “are you wearing suntan lotion?” way if that makes sense. The opening is amazing, I love the fruits, especially the lime. I think the lime sealed the deal for me actually. It stays for a little while then you get a more floral somewhat musky/powdery fragrance, from the tiare flower but not overly so as I don’t enjoy extremely floral scents.<br />
<br />
Projection is moderate. If you’re in someone’s bubble you’ll definitely smell them. It’s not a skin scent but not beast mode either. I tried this from a sample btw so a FB might preform better when I can do my overspray technique. It lasts a lot longer than most LV fresh scents I’ve tried though. I really want to buy afternoon swim but it only lasts less than 2 hours on me :( , this is much much better. I’d say a good 6-7 hours total with the first 3 hours being the most noticeable in silage to you and others. I don’t mind respraying though because the opening is my favorite part! It’s very uplifting and just puts me in a good mood.<br />
<br />
I went ahead and bought a bottle before the prices go up even more. Do I think it’s worth the $300 US dollars? For me, yes because like I said I was looking for a scent like this for awhile now. I don’t own a lot of beach vibe scents because I don’t live anywhere near anything that resembles the tropics lol, I’m in the Midwest. If I lived somewhere tropical I’d probably own more scents like this. Also like I mentioned, I was on the hunt for a beach scent that didn’t just remind me of sun tan lotion alone and the performance is good for what it is. This checks all the boxes for me but I could see why someone would think this is overhyped/overpriced though I can’t see someone not enjoying the scent overall, even if it is overpriced. It’s mass appealing. To me this a little slice of paradise. It transports me out of Kansas and to a beautiful beach. And can I just mention how much I loved the opening again? 😀 When I wore the sample I got a few compliments as well. I’m excited to receive my full bottle that I know I’ll put to good use this summer. ☀️</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="1556937"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=1556937#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1556126" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1363028">V.Scent.Orient</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-01">05/01/22 02:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>𝐋𝐮𝐱𝐮𝐫𝐲 𝐛𝐞𝐚𝐜𝐡 &amp; 𝐜𝐨𝐚𝐬𝐭 𝐥𝐢𝐟𝐞𝐬𝐭𝐲𝐥𝐞 ⛱️<br />
<br />
One of my favorite scent profile is a tropical beachy fragrance with dominant combination of citrus, white floral and also coconut accords to create a fresh beachy holiday vacation atmosphere. Today I will share about my latest love on this genre that has the best aspects the scent profile without becoming to holiday-iss so it can be enjoyed in everyday situations. Commonly beachy fragrance tend to create a fun holiday vibe that I only find appropriate to wear in recreational situation or mood especially in daytime activities. <br />
<br />
In 𝗖𝗜𝗧𝗬 𝗢𝗙 𝗦𝗧𝗔𝗥𝗦 the beachy tropical vibe is definitely present but it's sitting in a distance. The main stars of the show in the forefront here is the tiare flowers which is a little indolic, very creamy, bright and also fruity at the same time. And what separate this from others is it doesn't have coconut accords that tend come out as a sun tan lotion smells in this genre. <br />
<br />
The whole profile give a strong beachside cityscape vibe in a luxurious atmosphere exactly found in the city of Los Angeles where everyone is living the lifestyle but also working there. I can see this fragrance being worn 24/7 because it's an uplifting one but also can accommodate laid back situations perfectly. <br />
<br />
This has now become my most favorite fresh citrus floral because it can put me in feelings of a successful person and celebrity who lives or travels in L.A. It give the wearer ultimate feeling of joy and  optimism to pursue even the wildest dream. <br />
<br />
I highly recommend everyone to try this one because it's not only the best LV creations I've sampled but also amongst other brands in this genre for it's versatility to be worn anytime regardless of the weather.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1235347">nikath</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-20">04/20/22 14:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have been searching for a more delicate scent suitable for spring/summer and this is it!! City of Stars smells so juicy and delicious with the blood orange, lemon and lime as the most prominent notes of the opening followed by creamy, floral coconut on a slightly powdery classic LV-musky base. It is definitely reminiscent of the other citruses in the LA-inspired collection and is the one that leans most towards feminine marketed scents, as it dries down to the smell of a luxurious tropical balm. The sales assosiant told me there even is honey in here which I cannot confirm anywhere online, but I did find a source that stated there is a blend of orange flower, jasmine and coconut in here to mimic the scent of monoi oil. Performance is rather intimate as expected from a citrus fragrance so this is a scent that needs to be oversprayed and frequently reapplied if you want other people to notice it, obviously it is very overpriced but for me it just ticked all the boxes for what I was looking for scent-wise so I was willing to take the splurge.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755">The Wolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-10">04/10/22 02:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I find the LV house to be underwhelming and more hype than substance. <br />
However, they hit the the mark on this one. <br />
This opens up with super bright citruses, especially lime which I love. <br />
<br />
The burst of lime reminds me of Virgin Island Water ( although not on good) and then transitions to bergamot and orange. Opening and mid are excellent 👌 <br />
Once you get to the base you get tiare, creamy powder and musk which forms a very nice suntan lotion. <br />
<br />
Unlike the other warm weather frags from Luis Vuitton, this one has strong performance. <br />
The suntan lotion doesn't have coconut, so it's more like a high end sunscreen. <br />
Might be redundant if you already have a suntan lotion fragrance, but if not this one is worth looking into. <br />
<br />
Scent 8/10<br />
Performance 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="1540489"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=1540489#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1540450" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249347">Chesco</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-09">04/09/22 23:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So i finally got my hands on this gorgeous bottle.<br />
First spray blind buy review.<br />
<br />
A fruit salad of 5 citruses + a bunch of white florals (heliotrope and jasmine ‘i think’ 🤔) + a light creaminess to the florals + a light wood (either sandlewood or cedar or Iso E Super).<br />
<br />
You know what hit my brain immediately when smelling it?  Initio’s ‘Musk Therapy’!<br />
Makes sense as the recent exposure had created a beloved small hype with that fragrance and i can see competitors trying to copy it to add it as an offering to their customers and to take some of Initio’s profits.<br />
<br />
But this fragrance ‘City of Stars’ has more prominent citrus and stronger floral smelling flowers vs ‘Musk Therapy’, and is not as elegant, and because of this, it does projects more off the skin.  <br />
<br />
Im not a fan of the florals chosen for this frag as they smell cheap &amp; dated.  But i love the florals in ‘Musk Therapy’ - they are elegantly added, soft feminine, submissive and Sunday relaxing gorgeous.  ‘Musk Therapy’ also takes a few wearings to understand the dna, smell it other than a skin scent and to appreciate it’s unique soft beauty.  With ‘City of Stars’ you understand the dna 🧬 right away on first wearing.<br />
<br />
It doesn’t smell anything quite new and i think it’s LV’s version of ‘Musk Therapy’, and not as good imo.  <br />
<br />
Nice fragrance for the High-heat Spring.  But again the dated floral ruined it for me as it’s the cloying kind of floral.  :/<br />
<br />
3/5 Woofs</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="1540450"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=1540450#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1540424" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; On me, it opens with juicy bergamot, and then, I guess due to the musk and powdery notes, settles into a very fancy luxe citrus-scented dryer sheet/freshly laundered sheets at a very luxe hotel type thing. I kind of love that about it. I feel that it is one of the most unisex fragrances I have ever tried.<br />
<br />
Edit: I don’t know if my nose has changed or if my allergies are less severe, but I get more of the vibrant, juicy, and slightly sweet citrus in the opening now than I did before. I don’t experience this as a distinctly powdery fragrance; it doesn’t have any makeup-y quality, which is good because I hate powdery fragrances. The drydown still strikes me as slightly luxe dryer sheets but less than it did before.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="73344"comment_id="1540009"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/City-Of-Stars-73344.html?ccid=1540009#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1539869" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; In the end the citrusy notes only lasted about an hour and a half on me. <br />
<br />
Once the initial citrusy blast had faded, the sweet and slightly fruity and tropical white flower known as tiare began to unfurl deliciously on my skin and envelop me. I could get a good dose of the musk as well followed by the powdery notes and the sandalwood in that order, but the tiare flower in this was really what shone to me.<br />
<br />
I feel like I'm on a tropical vacation in the Pacific Islands in this and it makes me feel like a tropical island goddess. This is why I definitely think a woman could wear it during the day in both spring and especially summer.<br />
<br />
Heures D'Absence had a moderate sillage on me and it lasted on my skin for  about 10 hours surprisingly. Because of this and the rest above, I'd give this perfume an excellent 8/10.
